<|begin_of_text|>
Pergunta: apresente os top 2 containers Docker que mais consomem RAM
Resposta:
{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:2]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:9]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:6]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:5]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:8]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:10]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:3]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

Resposta:
{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:5]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:10]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>

{"command":"docker stats --no-stream --format '{{ json . }}' | jq -s 'sort_by(.MemPerc | sub(\"%\"; \"\") | tonumber) | reverse | .[:5]'","risk":false}
<|end_of_text|>
